== Budiriro yekudhindwa kwezvinyorwa zvake ==
'''Chiokisitani''' (kureva ''Occitan''; ''lenga d'òc;'' [[Chifurenji]]: ''langue d'oc'') kana '''Chilen'a dhi-oku''' nevatauri vekuzvarwa. Chiokisitani mutauro we [[Chirhoma]] unotaurwa ku[[Chamhembe che Furanzi|Chamhembe kwe Furanzi]], [[Monako]], [[Mipata ye Okisitani]] ye [[Itari]], uyezve ne [[Vhari Dhi'Arani]] ye [[Speini]]; zvichiunganidzwa pamwe zvisi izvi zinodananwa dzimwe nguva sa Okisitaniya. Chiositani chinotaura mu [[Kalabhiriya]] ([[Chamhembe che Itari]]) mumankilavhu eururimi eruwa re[[Kosenza]] (kazhinji [[Guardia Piemontese]]). Vamwe vanosanganisa [[Chikatala]] muChiokisitani, nekuti [[Nhambwe ye Ururimi|nhambwe]] yemutauro uyu ne mitauronyina imwe ye Chiokisitani (senge mutauro we [[Chigaskoni]]) wakafana nenhambwe wemitauronyina ye Chiokisitani. Chikatala chainoonekwa semutauronyina weChiokisitani kusvika kupera kwe [[Zanagore rechiGuminepfumbamwe]] uye nhasi uchiri mutauro unehukama huri pedyo nawo.

Vamwe vagari vemuBulawayo vanoti havachawone kukosha kwegungano remabhizimisi rinoitwa pagore rega rega reZimbabwe Internatiomnal Trade Fair kana kuti ZITF, iro ratanga muguta reBulawayo neChipiri. Vamwe vagari vataura neStudio 7 vati gungano reZITF raivapa mukana wekuti vaende nemhuri dzavo kunoona zvakasiyana siyana kuZITF asi vati mamiriro akaita zvinhu munyaya dzezvehupfumi ave kuita kuti vasaona kukosha kwechiitiko ichi. Mumwe weavo vataura neStudio 7 ndemumwe mugari uyo angozvidoma nezita rekuti Amai Tawonga. Amai Tawonga vati ZITF iri kuuya panguva iyo vari kutotemwa nemusoro kuti vabatanidze mari yekubhadharira vana vavo chikoro sezvo zvikoro zviri kuvhurwa svondo rinouya. Mumwewo mugari, Muzvare Clara Moyo, vati vanosiendawo nevana vavo kuTrade Fair asi vati pari zvino zvinhu zvakavawomera, vakatsinhirawo kuti vari mushishi rekutsvaga mari yechikoro yevana vavo. VaTaipanei Mutadza vaimboshandira imwe yaive kambani hombe yaigadzira mbatya muBulawayo asi yakazovhara. VaMutadza vati vaive mumwe wevashandi vekambani iyi vaigara vachienda kuTrade Fair kunoratidza zvinhu zvaigadzirwa nekambani iyi. VaMutadza vanoti ivo semunhu ave kuedza kutangawo kuzvishandira pachavo vega, vanoona gungano reZITF rakakosha sezvo richivapa mukana wekuwana mazano ebhizimisi kune vamwe. Mumashoko avo kuvatapi venhau muBulawayo, sachigaro weZITF, VaBekhithemba Nkomo, vati kunyange hazvo mamiriro ezvehupfumi munyika asina kumira zvakanaka, vari kufadzwa nezviratidzwa zviri pagungano reZITF regore rino vachiti zviratidzwa izvi ndezvemhando yepamusoro kupfuura mamwe makore mashoma apfuura. | align=center colspan=2 | [[File:Ghana (orthographic projection).svg|300px]]
true, anchor_year, COinS_date
The Wikimedia Foundation has named [[:mw:Wikimedia_Engineering/2014-15_Goals#Top_departmental_priorities_for_Q3_.28January-March_2015.29|its top priorities for this quarter]] (January to March). The first priority is making VisualEditor ready for deployment by default to all new users and logged-out users at the remaining large Wikipedias. You can help identify these requirements. <mark>There will be weekly '''triage meetings '''which''' will be open to volunteers''' beginning Wednesday, 11 February 2015 at [http://www.timeanddate.com/worldclock/fixedtime.html?iso=20150211T12&p1=224&ah=1 12:00 (noon) PST] (20:00 UTC). </mark> Tell Vice President of Engineering [[:foundation:User:Damon_Sicore_(WMF)|Damon Sicore]], Product Manager [[:mw:User:Jdforrester_(WMF)|James Forrester]] and other team members which bugs and features are most important to you. The decisions made at these meetings will determine what work is necessary for this quarter's goal of making VisualEditor ready for deployment to new users. The presence of volunteers who enjoy contributing MediaWiki code is particularly appreciated. Information about how to join the meeting will be posted at [[:mw:Talk:VisualEditor/Portal|mw:Talk:VisualEditor/Portal]] shortly before the meeting begins.

'''Zerere''' kana '''rumbihli''' ([[Chingezi|nge.]] ''green''), [[Mavara ekutanga|ruvara rwokutanga]], uye huri pakati pe[[Ungu (Ruvara)|ungu]] ne[[Huroro (Ruvara)|huroro]] pane [[nangazira]] inovonekwa. Zerere ndeumwe [[muvara]] wokutanga pamwechete ne mu[[tsvuku]] ne mu[[ungu]], unowedzerwa pakusanganisa kuti mamwe mavara agadzirwe. Nezvakakurakwazvo, ruvara rwe zerere runowanikwa muzvisikwa senge [[chimbishidza]]<ref group="C">'''chlorophyll.,''' kutodza 「''rumbishi''」rimwe zita rokuti zerere; chiro chimbishi chiro chinemuvara wezerere mumashure mekuibva.</ref>, nechemushonga inoshandiswa nemadzinde pa[[chirukanerujeko]] ne kushandura [[chiedza]] chezuva kuita simba rechemushonga. Zvisikwa zvakawanda zvino shanduka kutora karuvara kezerere kenharaunda sokuita [[chihwandekumhene]]<ref group="C">'''camouflage.,''' kuChishona chamazuva ose tingati 「''chihwandekumhene''」 uye tichitodza [[Chindau]] tingati 「''Chafihlakumhene'', ''chafishakumhene'' 」. Mashoko aya avambwa achitodza chirevo cheshoko ririkuturikirwa ndikokusanganiswa kwemashoko okuti 'kuviga, kufisha, kuhwanda' ne 'mhene, jeka, vheneka'.</ref>. [[Muchegwa|Michegwa]] yakawanda ine ruvara rwezerere, kusanganisira iyo [[murawudhi]]<ref group="C">'''emerald.,'''</ref>, inopihwa ruvara rwayo ne[[Chirochemo|chemo]]<ref group="C">'''content.,''' kureva 「''chirochemo'' 」 kana 「''chimo, chemo''」 pakupfupisa.</ref> chezerere ne[[rhangi]]<ref group="C">'''chromium., chroma...,'''</ref> rainaro.

Iyo yekupedzisira ndiyo basa rinokosha kupfuura dzose, sekuzorora kwemaitiro, masticatory nematauriro emashoko zvinokonzera kusununguka kukuru uye kunzwa kworugare. Zvimwe, manzwiro ekurwadziwa anokonzerwa: a) mumasanganisi emasticatory; b) mumisungo yekutaura (mitsipa yerurimi nemarara); c) mukufananidza misungo (misungo yemiromo, maziso, nheyo, pamberi). Zvadaro, mushure mekukwanisa kufungidzira kusuruvara mumatumbo ose, kunouya kunzwa kwokuzorora zvakakwana uye kunyorova kuneta.
